Reader's Advisor

㈠ How to Strive Out of a Corrupt Family 160

Letter from Mr. Liu Youwei

After reading Mr. Song Shize’s letter and your reporter’s response in today’s newspaper, I have the following thoughts: ㈠ In the current social situation, corrupt families of feudal remnants cannot be fundamentally eradicated; thus, Mr. Song’s problem will not be fundamentally solved. ㈡ Advising Mr. Song’s mother to find a job and support herself is certainly a proper method, but when it comes to finding a job, "how easy is it?" Now, many college graduates cannot find a job that pays twenty or thirty yuan a month. Where would a middle-aged, dull, old-fashioned woman find a job? If Mr. Song wants to break away from her, it seems inhumane. ㈢ Mr. Song's father and his concubine are indeed "living in the old society, within the category of feudal remnants." Suicide is out of the question, so the only option is to let them "sit and wait for death." This is a painful solution, but in today's society, there are probably quite a few people like Mr. Song's parents. If we listen to them and let them live or die on their own, that is not the attitude that people who study social problems should have. What do Mr. Song and your reporter think about this?

Answer: What you said in your letter is insightful. However, when we study social problems, especially with readers who are studying pressing personal problems, we should divide it into two steps: The first step is to contribute some practical solutions within our limited knowledge so that readers will not be disappointed and feel their questions are not answered. The second step is that if every practical problem is solved only from the practical, individual phenomena, ignoring its social and economic root causes, that is, the motive force of the motive force, then although the reader has obtained a considerable solution, the social root cause has not been fundamentally solved. Therefore, readers should be reminded at any time and place so that everyone does not only focus on the individual phenomena of reality and forget the causes and common connections behind this phenomenon. Yesterday's reply to Mr. Song was only to provide some insights on the urgent problems he needed to solve. As for Mr. Song's family situation, it is still a large part of China, at least a common phenomenon in a large part of the old society. Solving this problem cannot be achieved overnight. If you really want to help, then at least the following conditions are required: ㈠ National capitalization or national industrialization under the people's regime; ㈡ Strict punishments should be used to implement the prohibition of opium, and it should not be expressly prohibited while secretly encouraged; Concubinage is strictly prohibited; Those who take concubines shall not enjoy civil rights; ㈣ The state should use all its efforts to implement universal education, and secondary school education should be completely funded by the state. Students should be free of charge regardless of class or gender: ㈤ People should be unconditionally allowed to have freedom of assembly, association and publication, so that people's intelligence and talent can be fully developed, so as not to submerge and thwart people's interest and mood in striving upwards: ㈥ The right to education of young students and young children has absolute protection. If they are out of school at the age of study, their fathers and brothers should be severely punished. There must be a major upheaval to stir up a social upheaval, which is absolutely unimaginable under the current political and economic situation. This is why the reporter temporarily ignores and disregards the problem of rescuing Mr. Song's father and his concubine. As for the reporter's suggestion that Mr. Song should break away from her when it is absolutely necessary (if she does not listen to his advice), it seems wrong, but in fact, it is all based on the standpoint of the entire society. If Mr. Song lives with his mother, both of them will have no way out. For the sake of the future of society, temporarily abandoning Mr. Song's mother and letting Mr. Song get rid of it is also the meaning of "weighing the two evils and taking the lesser." This may cause the old men in the Minglun Hall to sigh and criticize it! What do you think?

㈡ This is a Social Problem 161

Letter from Mr. Zhu Ying

(Regarding the discussion on the economic oppression issue raised by Mr. Weng, Mr. Weng's original letter and Mr. Zhu's discussion letter can be found in this column on October 19th and 22nd)

I am generally satisfied with the points you answered. However, since your newspaper has a special column to solve some difficult problems for readers, everyone is happy to hear the news when they have any doubts, and once your newspaper replies, they will follow it like a needle, thinking that there will be a solution in the future. Therefore, your newspaper should be careful in its statements. If it can partially solve the problem, it should help solve it. Otherwise, it should tell him other ways out, or at least withhold judgment! For example, in your newspaper's reply to Mr. Weng, it says: "As long as you can endure hardship, you will not starve to death." In the current Chinese society, this sentence seems too affirmative. You should know that even in Shanghai, which seems to be very prosperous on the surface, if a hard-working poor person does not rely on the support of relatives and friends, I am afraid that many people will starve to death! If you, sir, are willing to make in-depth observations, you will know. From this point of view, if Mr. Weng believes it to be true after receiving your newspaper's reply, and if he loses his principal's job in the future and tries hard to find a job, either the factory will not add people, or it will not want novices. Or even if he finds a job, the factory will either close down due to the influence of the current situation, or he will be exhausted all day long due to the result of rationalizing production and will not get enough to eat. At this time, although Mr. Weng's family did not starve to death, they were half-dead from starvation; when he had no choice, he had to take the path of suicide; on the one hand, it made society distrust your newspaper's guidance. If your newspaper had clearly told Mr. Weng from the beginning: "This is a problem for the entire society. To solve your individual problem, you have to solve the entire society. As for solving the urgent needs of the moment, it is not without merit, but it is just 'treating the head when it hurts and treating the foot when it hurts'." If you are willing to turn your head around and say this, Mr. Weng may shift his focus to transforming society, so that he will not waste his energy in vain, and it is also your newspaper's true fulfillment of its guiding mission. In short, the current society is not a problem of "having or not having", but a problem of "distribution". I hope that your newspaper will tell the masses this without ambiguity.

I am not argumentative, I hope your newspaper will be a star of society, and a star for the eternal future. I wonder what your reporter thinks?

Reply: We are very happy that you are willing to discuss with us repeatedly. You talked about: We should have clearly told Mr. Weng from the beginning: "This is a problem for the entire society," and called him to focus on transforming society from the beginning. In fact, this meaning has been hidden in our original reply to Mr. Weng, but the wording is slightly obscure. I have already explained the rest in the previous letter, so I will not repeat it here. I respectfully acknowledge all your instructions!

Page 11

Education News

Junior High School Curriculum Standards (12) 162

Music

First, Objectives

(1) To develop students' musical talents and interests.

(2) To enable students to sing common simple and compound songs and understand basic music theory.

(3) To train hearing so that they can appreciate ordinary famous songs.

(4) To cultivate beautiful emotions and the spirit of harmony, medicinal groups, striving, and progress.

Second, Time Allocation

(1) First academic year, two hours per week.

(2) Second and third academic years, one hour per week each.

(3) In the first academic year, the prescribed lecture time for music theory is 30 minutes per week, and the remaining time is used to teach singing. In the second and third academic years, the prescribed lecture time for music theory is 20 minutes per week, and the remaining time is used to teach singing.

Third, Teaching Material Outline

(1) First academic year,

㈠ Music Theory 1. Reading music, A. Organization of sheet music, various symbols on the staff regarding the pitch (staff), length (note rests), strength (beat), speed (tempo) of the sound, etc.

B. Scales, major scales (or major scales) and their cognate minor scales (or minor scales) and their cognate keys, C. Modulation, identification of modulations to nearby keys, 2. General knowledge of music, A. Meaning of music, B. Overview of music development, C. Classification of music, D. Human voice and vocal music,

㈡ Singing 1. Basic exercises, A. Vocal exercises, pronunciation exercises), B. Tone exercises (C major, G major, F major, D major, Bb major), C. Interval exercises (second interval, third interval, fourth interval), 2. Songs A. Single-tone songs B. Duet songs,

(2) Second academic year

㈠ Music Theory 1. General knowledge of music (continuing from the previous academic year, A. Musical instruments and instrumental music, B. Classical music and Romantic music, C. Absolute music and program music, D. Music and life, 2. Introduction to Harmony, A. Intervals and their types, B. Construction and classification of triads, C. Organization of four parts, D. Rules for connecting triads, E. Two major prohibitions in harmonic progression,

㈡ Singing 1. Basic exercises, A. Vocal and pronunciation exercises, etc., B. Scale exercises (same as the previous academic year), C. Tone exercises (A major, Eb major, A minor, E minor, D minor), D. Interval exercises (fifth interval, sixth interval)

(3) Third academic year

㈠ Music Theory 1. Introduction to Harmony (continuing from the previous academic year), A. Inversion of triads, B. Rules for sixth chords and four-six chords, C. Construction and classification of seventh chords, D. Rules for resolving dominant seventh chords, E. Inversion of seventh chords (five-six chord, three-four chord, two chord), F. Modulation and cadence, G. Harmonic analysis of musical works, H. Application of Harmony, 2. Small song composition (in extracurricular teaching), ㈡ Singing 1. Basic exercises, A. Scale exercises (same as the previous academic year), B. Tone exercises (Eb major changing to A major, Bb minor, G minor), C. Interval exercises (seventh interval, octave interval), 2. Songs, A. Duet songs, B. Trio songs C. Simple quartet songs, ㈢ Instrumental music (in extracurricular teaching) 1. Introduction to playing the organ, 2. Introduction to playing the piano 3. Introduction to playing the violin, 4. Playing Chinese instruments such as erhu, sanxian, pipa, yueqin, shengxiao, flute, etc.), Note: Students may choose one of the above instruments to learn as needed,

Fourth, Summary of Implementation Methods

(1) Homework Requirements,

㈠ Singing is divided into "basic exercises" and "songs" for teaching.

㈡ Music theory is divided into "reading music", general knowledge of music, and "introduction to harmony" for teaching, but if necessary, a "small song composition method" may be added.

㈢ For instrumental music, students choose one of the organ, piano, violin, and national instruments to learn extracurricularly, but it may be temporarily absent due to school equipment difficulties and other circumstances.

(2) Teaching Points,

㈠ From now on, the movable-do solfège method should be eliminated and replaced with the fixed-do solfège method currently used in various countries (the Ministry of Education is compiling a summary of the theory of the fixed-do solfège method and an elaboration of the comparison of the advantages and disadvantages of the movable-do solfège method).

㈡ Special attention should be paid to basic exercises in singing, because general students often neglect them because they are not pleasing to the ear, so teachers must sincerely guide them.

㈢ Basic exercises must be performed within five or ten minutes before each singing, and the last five minutes must be used to sing songs that have been sung well or are particularly loved. ㈣ The sheet music must be completely in staff notation and absolutely no numbered notation should be used. ㈤ When selecting teaching materials, it is advisable to select more majestic and lively songs. If you are inclined to sad and frequent songs, it is best to use them less except when necessary, and all decadent sounds must be eliminated.

㈥ Regardless of single or multiple tones, it is best to select songs with accompaniment. When teaching, the teacher should also use playing accompaniment as the standard. In this way, students can develop the habit of listening to polyphony while singing, so as to increase their appreciation of music. However, after the new song is sung well, they must develop the habit of singing alone without musical instruments.

㈦ When students sing, pay attention to their pronunciation, mouth shape, attitude, expression, etc., and correct them at any time.

㈧ Pay attention to the common range of students. If students are in the "changing voice period", they should be temporarily suspended from singing.

㈨ The division of parts for multiple-tone singing must be determined based on the total number of students, gender, and individual range. Generally, girls sing high notes and boys sing low notes. As for trio and quartet choral pieces, both boys and girls must be divided into two parts, but in schools where there are particularly few girls or where boys and girls are separated, special attention must be paid to the division of parts.

㈩ Long-scale keys should be used more often for songs, and short-scale keys should be used less often.

㈩㈠ Students should be required to sing songs faithfully, and it is strictly forbidden to add tunes and glissandos at will, so that the fun of teaching songs will flow into baseness.

㈩㈡ When lecturing on "reading music", in addition to enabling students to read music, they must also practice writing music, and they must also practice "dictation" within a considerable period of time.

㈩㈢ When lecturing on "general knowledge of music", it is advisable to prepare more famous records of vocal and instrumental music, and use the phonograph at any time so that students can have more opportunities to appreciate them. When famous musicians perform and concerts are held locally, they must be required to attend.

㈩㈣ When lecturing on "harmony", it is advisable to refer to and explain actual musical works at any time.

㈩㈤ Students with special talents can be asked to learn musical instruments (such as organ, piano, etc.) extracurricularly, and "small song composition methods" can be lectured on when necessary to allow them to try to compose simple songs.

Special Article

Local News

The Municipal Education Bureau Orders All Schools Not to Use Exaggerated Words for Publicity 164

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued an order yesterday to all private secondary schools, stating that according to Yu Ziyu, the principal of the private Southeast Women's Physical Education Normal School, in his presentation of opinions on rectifying private schools, many physical education schools in Shanghai use publicity as a tool for enrollment, such as placing advertisements and submitting news articles about the number of lectures given at certain places, the construction of school buildings, gymnasiums, sports fields, and swimming pools, etc., and also organizing teams to reach South America and the Americas, etc., all of which are promoted in this way. In fact, the so-called school buildings are only two or three residential houses, and as for the track and field, there is not even a running track, let alone other equipment. It goes without saying that students who live far away in other provinces do not know the truth and are deceived by such news. The bureau should issue a notice to all newspapers that such self-submitted publicity news must be verified before it is allowed to be published, so as not to deceive students from afar. According to this investigation, some private schools have been recruiting new students recently, and some of them specialize in publicity and do not focus on practical matters, which is originally inappropriate. In the future, when all schools publish enrollment advertisements, issue enrollment brochures, printed materials, etc., they must be realistic and truthful, and they must not use exaggerated words for publicity. If they dare to violate this deliberately, they will be severely punished once they are found to be in violation. This order is hereby notified.

Recent News on the Construction of the Municipal Zoo 169

Second Phase of Construction is Underway

Opening on New Year's Day is Not True

The Municipal Zoo on Wenmiao Road in this city has been under construction since the bidding, and it has been four months. The first phase of the project was fully completed at the beginning of this month. The second phase of the project, such as piling up artificial mountains, repairing the banks of the pool, installing water pipes and lights, and paving grass and planting trees, etc., has also been half completed. The unfinished part is currently in active progress. In addition, due to factual needs, a peacock pavilion and a mixed poultry house have been added outside the scope of the first two phases of the project. The mixed poultry house is built on the edge of the pool, half on land and half in water. The project is more difficult to carry out and will probably not be completed until the end of January next year. The previous rumor that it would open on New Year's Day is not true.

The addition of classes will still be done according to the previous discussion. ㈡ Fang Er Primary School requested to hire an assistant teacher and increase the subsidy. Decision: It is difficult to approve because it involves changing the budget. ㈢ How should the Shanghai Office of this bureau be relocated after the treatment? 8,000 Fans Overjoyed and Ecstatic: Donghua Defeats Western Concessions Police 4-2 176

Comparison of the Strengths of the Two Teams 177

Tung Wah: Iron Gate Zhou Xianyan, dressed in a traditional Chinese robe and mandarin jacket yesterday, looking refined and scholarly, sat in the one-dollar seats with his beloved Ms. Zhang Chunxun. When asked why he wasn't playing in such a big match, Zhou replied that he had injured his shin in a previous game against Lancashire and hadn't fully recovered. Therefore, in yesterday's match, A-Lu (Zhong En) took his place. Forward Chen Hongguang was also unable to play due to a foot injury, so Wan Xianghua filled the left inside forward position. Spectators on the left were worried about Tung Wah's lineup. However, once the fierce battle began, Tung Wah's strength not only didn't suffer the slightest loss, but the entire team seemed invigorated, with a solid formation. The forwards ran quickly, breaking through defenses and threatening the goal, often catching the opponent off guard. Chen Jiaqiu, in particular, was well-liked, achieving everything he desired. Xianghua and Jingyong were small and nimble, perfectly suited to their roles. Center Li Yichen's footwork was sharp and his shots were quick, but he tended to delay when dribbling and passing. The three halfbacks and two fullbacks were all outstanding, doing their best to control the enemy, creating an impenetrable defense, full of fighting spirit. Even the strong Western Police forwards couldn't find a weakness. Goalkeeper A-Lu had long been famous at sea for catching high balls, but yesterday he not only demonstrated his mastery of high balls but also handled low balls with ease. In short, yesterday's Tung Wah had a well-organized formation and an unusually full spirit.

Western Police: Yesterday's Western Police seemed slightly weaker in their fighting ability. It was a pity that they lacked shooting talent; even when they reached the goal, it was in vain. Individually, right fullback Crawford was indeed weak, with soft footwork and unable to intercept the enemy's advances. Halfback Hurley ran tirelessly but to no avail, allowing Chen Jiaqiu to advance freely and unhindered, which was a major loss and weakness for Western Police. Among the forwards, Wakenshaw was the most outstanding, displaying the demeanor of an experienced veteran. Wu Youliang and Guan Xun'an were not easy to stop. Whenever Western Police attacked, the ball invariably came up the left side, with excellent crosses, almost never missing. Unfortunately, the central support was weak, resulting in wasted efforts. Duffy, a talented halfback, was reassigned to inside forward, acting like a headless fly, unsure of what to do. Pike, Jackson, and Oakley were still respectable but couldn't score. The mainstay of Western Police, center-half Kasha, surprisingly lost his nerve yesterday, his veteran reputation crumbling into confusion. His panicky state contributed to Western Police's defeat, making him partly to blame.

A Glimpse of the Competitive Situation 178

Western Police Have Terrible Luck: Western Police conceded a goal within two minutes of the start of the match, and this loss must be attributed to Kasha's mishandling, heading the ball into his own net. This was an omen of Western Police's failure. Otherwise, how could they have accurately thrown themselves into the net during such an important match, destroying their own prestige? This was one of Western Police's major misfortunes. After conceding this goal, Western Police certainly didn't resign themselves to weakness; they worked hard and actively counterattacked, surrounding Tung Wah's goal, firing shots like a string of firecrackers for more than ten minutes. Wakenshaw delivered four or five excellent corner kicks in a row, and Jackson and Pike had five or six shots, but they achieved nothing. This was Western Police's second major misfortune. The ineffective siege allowed Tung Wah to score another goal. This was Western Police's third major misfortune. After much hard work and repeated efforts, they finally scored a goal in return. Shortly after, they had a penalty kick opportunity, which could have easily turned their hatred into joy and transformed danger into safety, creating a 2-2 tie. However, Kasha's kick was saved by Tung Wah goalkeeper Lu Zhongen, missing the opportunity and destroying his own prestige. Otherwise, after creating a 2-2 tie, the subsequent situation would have been completely different, and the outcome might have been reversed. This was Western Police's fourth major misfortune. With these four points, it can be said that they had terrible luck.

Tung Wah Were Pleasantly Surprised: Tung Wah had a good start, with luck shining upon them. Western Police besieged their goal but failed to score, and A-Lu saved the penalty kick. This was Tung Wah's good fortune and blessing. Kasha scored an own goal, but even though Western Police had terrible luck, they could still remedy the situation with the subsequent penalty kick. However, Kasha failed, preventing them from achieving a 2-2 tie. In the second half, they conceded another goal and then another, losing repeatedly. Western Police's courage was lost, and they had no choice but to lose. Tung Wah were pleasantly surprised and overjoyed. Tung Wah can be called lucky. They have a high chance of winning the Group A championship this year. However, being lucky is one thing; high performance requires a solid formation and strong combat power to achieve this.

The Fierce Battle of the First Half 179

Kasha Scores Own Goal: As the bell rang three times and referee Marshall blew the whistle, the battle began. Tung Wah kicked off and advanced a few steps, but Western Police counter-pressed. Jackson dribbled forward, but Li Ning intercepted. Kasha and Wan Xianghua both lost their footing, and Qian Jingyong got the ball and pressed toward the goal. Blocked by Crawford, he passed it in front of the goal. The ball grazed the goal to the right. Li Yichen, Chen Jiaqiu, and the Western Police goalkeeper all missed it. Chen Jiaqiu caught up and shot at the goal. In a panic, Kasha crashed into the ball, mistakenly hitting it into his own net. Tung Wah received this unexpected joy, and the surrounding spectators were overjoyed. It was less than two minutes from the start of the match, which can be described as extremely fast.

Full of Storms: Western Police were extremely frustrated by this misfortune, so they reorganized their forces and launched a rapid counterattack. From then on, Tung Wah's goal was besieged, full of storms, with everyone on edge. Oakley crossed the ball into the center, and Jackson headed it, but the ball grazed the left side. Wakenshaw's attempt to sneak through failed and was saved by Guan Xun'an. Western Police missed their first opportunity. Wakenshaw refused to give up and dribbled the ball forward again, passing it to Duffy, who passed it to Pike. This gentleman's shot was too high, missing their second opportunity. Hurley won a corner kick. Wakenshaw made a beautiful cross, and Lu Zhongen jumped up to save it. Western Police missed their third opportunity. Wakenshaw delivered another corner kick, but it was again saved by A-Lu. Western Police missed their fourth opportunity. Wakenshaw relied on his lifelong heroism to invade alone, crossing the ball from a suitable position. Jackson was in a good position, seemingly poised for success, but Tu Kaiyuan, seeing the opportunity was not good, chased and intercepted. Thus, Western Police missed their fifth opportunity. Finally, Western Police attacked for the sixth time. Oakley crossed the corner kick, and Wu Youliang blocked Wakenshaw's action and cleared the danger. Pike shot at the goal but it was caught. After all, Western Police were flawless. Western Police had launched seven attacks, creating a strong momentum. Tung Wah's goal was momentarily uneasy. Tung Wah resisted the invaders, flawlessly, which surprised and delighted the spectators.

Attempted Theft Failed: The more intense the pressure, the fiercer the resistance. After enduring the pressure for a long time and turning danger into safety, Tung Wah launched a counterattack. Yu Tian advanced along the side and passed to Jiaqiu, who shot at the goal, very urgently. The goalkeeper blocked it out. Western Police attacked again. Li Ning lost his footing, and Pike sneaked in, but he also lost his footing, regretting it. After that, Jackson and Pike took turns attacking the goal, and Tung Wah saved them one by one. After a long time of melee, Oakley kicked out a corner kick. In the melee, Pike kicked the ball into the goal, but Duffy committed a foul. Therefore, the attempted theft failed and cost them dearly, causing a hollow joy.

The Situation in the Second Half 180

Exchanging Goals: The second battle began, and the melee lasted for ten minutes, with few highlights. Suddenly, Chen Chutian delivered a corner kick, and the Western Police goalkeeper lost his guard. Li Yichen waited in front of the goal and poked the ball into the net, giving Tung Wah a two-goal lead. Seeing the situation was not good, Western Police mobilized their entire army and tried to advance. Winger Oakley sent the ball in front of the goal, where it landed in the corner. Wakenshaw saw the ball and chased it, aiming at the shadow of the ball and heading it into the goal. The situation was very beautiful, making it 2-1.

Penalty Kick: Western Police were encouraged by this goal and their spirits were boosted. Crawford sent the ball forward. Wakenshaw dribbled forward, passed Li Ning, and was about to shoot at the goal, but he lost the opportunity due to his flustered footwork. Suddenly, the Western Police forwards pressed forward with their entire army. In the midst of the chaos, the Tung Wah defenders committed a foul, resulting in a penalty kick. Standing firm, Tung Wah goalkeeper A-Lu watched the opportunity calmly. Kasha ran forward and kicked hard, aiming the ball at the left corner of the goal. A-Lu had foreseen this and had already calculated this move, diving with both hands to turn it into a corner kick. Wakenshaw then kicked a wild ball, turning danger into safety, much to the surprise. The Tung Wah players ran forward to congratulate A-Lu, all overjoyed. In the blink of an eye, Yu Tian made a crisp kick, passing to Xiao Wan, who then passed it to Li Yichen, who swept the ball into the net, making the score 3-1.

Solo Effort: After being severely wounded, Kasha was unwilling to give up, so he reassigned Pike to center forward, planning to make a desperate last stand, but to no effect. Suddenly, a loud cry was heard from the right flank. It was Chen Jiaqiu making a solo effort, rushing forward on horseback, dribbling past three defenses, and shooting hard at the goal. Edmon was helpless, only able to watch the incoming ball, like an arrow, shoot into the net, making the score 4-1.

Bullseye: By this point, Tung Wah's victory was already in their grasp, and the enemy's defense line was tired and exhausted, no longer as formidable as before. After a time of melee, there was still no progress. Pike was assisted by Hui Siwu, dribbling west, passing the penalty line, and then passing to Jackson, who passed to…

Duffy. Wu Youliang and Guan Xun'an rushed over, but accidentally tripped Duffy on the penalty line, resulting in a free kick. About twenty yards from the goal, Kasha made a low shot, again aiming at the left corner of the goal. A-Lu did not have the foresight to save the penalty kick, and the ball pierced the net. Not long after the kickoff, the final whistle blew.

Commercial News

Finance 187

China Bank Open as Usual During Winter Solstice Holiday

Silver Dollar and Auxiliary Coins Rates Steady

The day before yesterday, the silver market was particularly quiet due to the customs closure and the weekly holiday. However, yesterday, only foreign banks on the Bund were closed. Among the Chinese businesses, only China Communications and Communications followed suit. The Central Bank and other Chinese banks operated as usual, so the closure of banks was different from the past. The new customs office handled import and export taxes as usual, so commercial loans circulated without hindrance. However, due to the foreign banks' closure, import transactions could not be shipped due to the inability to transfer funds. Although Chinese banks were open as usual, they were not as busy as usual. The money market also traded as usual. The morning price of foreign currency was 7 yuan 1 fen 4 li and a half, and the afternoon price was 7 yuan 1 fen 4 li 6 hao and two and a half hu. The result was a half-li improvement. The amount of exchange drafts was 855,000 in the morning and 685,000 in the afternoon. Banknotes were 45,000 in the morning and 20,000 in the afternoon. Off-exchange banknotes were 70,000 in the morning and 65,000 in the afternoon. Checks were 20,000 in the morning and 45,000 in the afternoon. Bank transactions were 500,000 in the morning and 400,000 in the afternoon. The silver dismantling rate was 2% in both the morning and afternoon. Chinese banks collected more than 4 million and stored 500,000. Money shops collected more than 5.7 million in foreign currency receipts and more than 3.1 million in silver currency receipts. The transaction volume of small money shops was more than 400,000. Jiangnan small foreign coins were 6 yuan 2 fen 3 li in the morning and 6 yuan 3 fen 8 li in the afternoon, which was 8 li more than the previous day. The transaction volume was 8,500 jiao in the morning and 14,500 jiao in the afternoon. Guangdong small foreign coins were 6 yuan 2 fen and 5 hao in the morning and 6 yuan 2 fen and 1 li in the afternoon. The transaction volume was 95,000 jiao in the morning and 65,000 jiao in the afternoon. Silver dollars remained unchanged at 393,500 wen.

Securities: Bond Prices Plummet by About Two Yuan 189

Selling Pressure Strong, Investor Sentiment Weak

February Futures Open Today

This Month's Futures Trading Halted

Yesterday (December 26), spot trading at the Chinese Securities Exchange was generally not open in the morning, and transactions were also extremely rare in the afternoon. December futures trading was halted to settle all procedures before delivery. Only January futures were traded. However, prices plummeted and trading was particularly active. Investor sentiment was extremely weak. Many small investors sold off their holdings vigorously. Tianjin banks also sold off a considerable amount. As a result, prices fell sharply when trading opened in the morning, and the market remained weak throughout the day. There was a gradual decline with no signs of improvement. However, the local financial industry remained calm, generally engaging in purchases. The trend slightly eased in the closing session. As a result, 20 Customs, Bonds, Unified Salt Tax, and 19 Customs all fell by about 2 yuan, and others fell by about 1.5 yuan. The total daily spot trading volume was 18,000 yuan. The January futures trading volume was 3.6 million yuan in the morning and more than 2.8 million yuan in the afternoon, totaling 6.435 million yuan, of which salt tax accounted for more than 1.7 million yuan, and unified tax and 20 Customs bonds each accounted for 8-900,000 yuan.

Short-Term Financial Dark Market Continues to Rise 190

The 20-year short-term financial public bonds that have been trading on the Securities Exchange for three weeks have seen extremely scarce spot circulation on the market. Due to supply and demand, prices have risen sharply. Although the highest recorded price on the exchange side is 66 yuan, the actual off-exchange settlement price has reached 72-73 yuan.

Most Yarn Merchants

Yarn and Cotton 191

Embrace a Bullish Approach...Opinions Held...

Believe that the Red Market in Spring

Has a Great Possibility of Rising

The cotton yarn market is slightly better, and the situation tends to be firm. Market prices initially fell and then rose. Due to the rise in raw cotton, investor sentiment is optimistic, and most speculators tend to be bullish, expecting the spring red market to recover. When the market price falls, buying interest rises. However, there are a large number of arbitrageurs, 6-7000 bales, speculating on the current month's tender yarn, selling for January and buying for February and March, earning about 6-7% interest. There are already 16-17,000 bales of 20-count yarn stockpiled in yarn warehouses, and the inventory is increasing daily.

(Lowest and Highest Tender Prices) The market opened before the tender. Due to reports of Japanese military disturbances in Rehe, the situation became increasingly tense, and investor sentiment fluctuated. Prices for all months fell by 6-7 qian. The 122 market gradually recovered, and as a result, prices for all months fell by 1, 2, 3, and 4 qian. It was heard in the afternoon that actual demand was sluggish, but cotton prices suddenly rose, causing yarn prices to rise. Prices for all months rose by 1, 4, 5, 6, and 7 qian. The total daily transaction volume was 14,400 bales. It was found that Changfeng sold 1,050 bales, Tongfu 500 bales, Gengfeng 450 bales, Shenji 300 bales, Yukang 300 bales, and Dafeng 300 bales. Xie Sheng bought 1,250 bales, Senkang 500 bales, Yiyu 500 bales, Yuda 350 bales, and Taichang 300 bales. The closing prices are listed below.

Cotton Market Advances

The General Environment is Conducive to Bullish Forces

The cotton market has turned firmer again, and most investors are optimistic. Due to the lack of spot goods and weak supply from various sources, it is rumored that a certain manufacturer's delivery volume this month is not large. The price of foreign cotton in Shanghai is still difficult to agree on. It is expected that there will still be room for price increases after the US cotton customs clearance. There is also a rising trend in the gold market. All these situations are conducive to bullish forces. As a result, the market atmosphere is tense. However, the world cotton industry is still in an era of oversupply, and the future is lacking in certainty.

(Zheng Standard Rises 3-5 qian) The market opened steadily before the Zheng Standard tender. The 23 market gradually rose, with prices for all months rising by 5 fen to 1.5 qian. There was some hedging in the afternoon. The market suddenly tightened, with prices for all months rising by 1.5 qian to 3-4 qian. The May price of 4 taels discovered a new high point. The total daily transaction volume was 56,200 dan. It was found that Changyu sold 1,900 dan, Changfeng 3,700 dan, Yuanda 3,000 dan, Gengfeng 1,300 dan, Changhe 1,200 dan, and Yifeng 1,200 dan. Xie Sheng bought 4,300 dan, Jifeng 1,400 dan, Dafu 2,100 dan, Zhenda 1,200 dan, and Yichang 2,400 dan. The closing prices are listed below.

(Liverpool) Spot transactions were good last week. Futures trading was sluggish due to the approaching holidays. Tin prices fell slightly, and bulls took some profits. Japanese merchants and hedgers also sold, but there was a lack of speculative demand, so even with buying by the industry, it was difficult to maintain. The Egyptian cotton market was quiet and trending firm.

Grain Arrival and Brisk Sales in the Rice Market 195

(South Shanghai) Sources are abundant, reaching over a hundred businesses. Retail sales remain flat, while wholesale sales improve. The Suzhou and Tongbang rice dealers have stagnant sales due to heavy inventory, so the situation has become weak. Fortunately, wholesale sales of thin rice have improved, and the market can still stabilize, otherwise it will also be affected by the abundant supply. The Changbang, Yinyuan, Yangdujian and other varieties remain stable.

(Xinzha) About twenty-five or six boats of Changzhou, Wuxi, and Xianzi rice have arrived. Sales in this street were initially sluggish but then became active. Arrivals and sales of thin rice are balanced, and the market is stable. Kunshan rice has a large inventory and the price is moderate. Yinyuan rice dealers are slightly active, and the situation continues to be strong. Arrivals and sales of Yangdujian rice are slow, and the price remains unchanged.

Kexian Rice Hoarding Becomes Active, Price Rises by One Dime 196

｜Fujian Rice Purchasing Still Strong｜

Yesterday, arrivals of Kexian rice were not brisk, but hoarding dealers suddenly became active, and market sentiment improved, raising the price by one dime. Fujian rice purchasing remains strong, with hoarding dealers and Fujian dealers competing to purchase, making the market quite lively. However, traders from the North China regions and Guangdong, due to the arrival of Hexia rice and falling prices, have shifted their attention to Hexia japonica and indica rice. Hexia rice has a large existing inventory and a strong supply. Now that it can be re-exported, arrivals are even more abundant, and the market has fallen due to oversupply. Given the large inventory in the mainland and the good harvest, prices are unlikely to rise. Kexian rice, on the other hand, has high taxes and reduced water levels, and traders are not active. There are few arrivals in Shanghai, and once hoarding becomes active, the market is expected to improve. Yesterday, 1,000 bags of Jiangxi machine-milled late rice were offered at prices ranging from $8.66 to $8.45, and 562 bags of Hunan machine-milled oil rice were offered at prices ranging from $8.945 to $8.75. In addition, 300 bags of red rough rice were offered at $0.74, and 78 bags of Wuhu machine-milled rice were offered at $10, which were purchased by hoarding dealers and Fujian dealers.

Spot Flour Lacks Standards, Prices Rise 197

Yesterday, the flour market showed a trend of becoming firmer and more stable across all months. The quoted prices for foreign wheat were up about a dime in Chicago and about two dimes in Canada. Although the market is closed, the general sentiment is stable. Because there are only two trading days left this month, the market must be closed. Tianjin dealers have good spot sales, so spot flour is still being traded, which is why the market is optimistic. For deferred contracts, the mills are not eager to sell. Since there is no activity in the spot foreign wheat market, there are no inquiries from outside speculators. However, there is considerable buying, so the market is very strong. Later, due to some profit-taking by Fufeng and Huafeng, the situation eased slightly. The current stable trend is purely due to the lack of spot flour. Near-term flour prices are bound to rise. When foreign wheat arrives in large quantities in the future, there will naturally be changes. As a result, this month's price is up one cent from the previous week, January is up 1.75 cents, February is up 2 cents, March is up half a cent, April is up 1.25 cents, and May is up 0.75 cents.

Wheat Market Boosted by Flour Market in the Afternoon 198

Yesterday, after the wheat futures market opened in the morning, it generally showed a hovering trend. There were few transactions in each month, because there were not many chips this year. Although the market makers had been taking profits last week, the number was still small. (It is heard that the Grain Exchange will follow the flour exchange example and allow factories to use passbooks for buying and selling, with amounts ranging from 7,000 to 10,000 taels.) The transactions were not without reason. In the afternoon, trading was slightly smoother, and the market became slightly tighter. Because the flour market was rising, market sentiment was also boosted. Considering that the market will soon be closed, there will not be much fluctuation. As a result, January remained unchanged, February was up one cent, March was up two cents, and April was up one cent.

Oilseeds and Miscellaneous Grains Show Improvement 199

｜Dalian Round Beans Are More Popular｜

｜London Market Declines｜

Yesterday, the oilseed and miscellaneous grain market showed improvement, and sales by various dealers were also good. As a result, small beans are tight, broad beans are active, and Dalian round beans are particularly popular, rising four jiao compared to the previous market. Of the 600 bags of Pudong broad beans offered, both Ningbo and Guangdong dealers purchased them. Of the 272 bags of Guantian specialty Chongcai green beans, both Nanyang and Guangdong dealers purchased them. Of the 35 bags of Zhuzhen rice, Guangdong dealers purchased them exclusively. Of the 200 bags of Gaoyou green beans purchased by Fujian dealers, the largest quantity of 1,300 bags of Jiangbei soybeans and five carts of Zhengyangguan soybeans were purchased by local factories. One cart of Dalian round beans was purchased by a local garden workshop. The white sesame market was also strong, with 148 bags of Guantian high-quality white sesame and 148 bags of Tushan white sesame all being purchased by local dealers. 100 bags of Nanjing white sesame were purchased by Guangdong dealers. Yangzhuang offered 240 bags of Bengbu white sesame and 281 bags of Guzhen clean sesame. The prices of peanuts and raw kernels also rose by a small amount. The buyers were local and Guangdong dealers. 300 bags of Shuanggou peanuts and 99 bags of Zhongxing peanuts were purchased by local dealers, while 120 tons of Shandong raw kernels and 100 bags of Tancheng raw kernels were all purchased by Guangdong dealers. In the oil market, raw oil prices rose slightly, while soybean oil was stable and did not fluctuate much. Furthermore, according to a London dispatch on the 24th, Chinese soybeans fell slightly, at £7 per ton (equivalent to 5.1 taels per 100 catties).

Sugar Market: Red and White Sugar Prices Rise Again 200

24 Coarse Granulated White Sugar Rises 7.5 Cents

Chaozhou Green Ground Price Rises 3-4 Jiao

Yesterday's sugar market suddenly tightened due to increased demand from purchasing households. In the morning, Changxing offered over 2,000 bags of 24 coarse granulated white sugar at $15.75. In the afternoon, Changxing offered another 1,000 bags at the exchange, with the price rising again to $15.8, up 7.5 cents from the previous day. The market for medium granulated white Huaxin goods was even tighter. The 20th was still offered at $15, and the 18th was quoted at $14.8, but no deal was made. Dutch red 8 was at $11.7, 9 was at $11.9, and 10 was at $12. The market was strong. Zhenxin Factory's newly produced Qibai in Shanghai was offered at $14.9 yesterday for several hundred bags, and later rose to $15. Of the 700-plus bags of new Chaozhou green that arrived the day before yesterday, over 500 bags were offered yesterday at prices ranging from $9 to $8.6. However, there were no goods of Gaoti Zhuangqing, and the price was about $9.2, so it had already risen by 2 jiao compared to the previous market. Furthermore, according to a Shantou dispatch, recent arrivals in Shantou have risen by 3-4 jiao. Tianjin Qing was offered again yesterday for 60 bags at prices ranging from $9.85 to $9.5, a slight increase from before.

Northern Goods: Longkou Vermicelli Arrivals Increase, Turning to Decline 201

Longkou vermicelli has become sluggish because the Hesheng ship arrived with over 3,000 bags the day before yesterday, and inventory has suddenly become sufficient. The market is sluggish, and traders are offering at $18.6. Market prices have also fallen by 2 jiao. Yesterday, the market was quoted at $18.8, and the trend is weak.

Seafood and Raw Flour Sales are Brisk 202

｜Abundant Production of Cuttlefish, but Sluggish Sales｜

(Raw Flour) Recently, business for Guangdong dealers has gradually become active. Places such as Hunan, Hubei, Fujian, and Guangdong are gradually consuming supplies, so the merchants' inventory is gradually being depleted, and each stall's sales are tightening. Yesterday, the market price was: True Fei Qilin brand at $8.85, Deer brand at $8.25, Green Pagoda, Three Fish, and National Flag brands at $6.1, and Three Shrimp Handprint at $4.05. With the inventory already low, the market is particularly brisk. If sales to customers do not decrease, there may be a further rise.

(Cuttlefish) This year's cuttlefish production in various regions is said to be abundant. However, sales are unusually sluggish, resulting in oversupply. The streets are full of inventory, and the market is difficult to improve. Currently, Ningyang large is sold at $28, Shengshan goods at $23, ordinary goods at around $20, and lower-quality goods can be purchased for $15-16.

Piece Goods: Huate呢 Vary in Strength 203

Huate呢 (woolen fabric) is very tight, but the market price varies in strength, as winter sales vary in briskness and are related to the amount of inventory in the market. Yesterday, Monday, checkered Huate呢 was the most popular, because there were no arrivals and the market lacked inventory. Plain dark gray Huate呢 was also in good condition, as it is suitable for cold weather sales, but prices were only slightly better, because the inventory was sufficient, so it was difficult to follow the rise. Colored Huate呢 supply and demand were equal, so there were no gains or losses. Because shimmering colors are not suitable for the season, they have mostly weakened.

Swallow Girl (3) 223

— Ye Lingfeng

After taking two more puffs of her cigarette, she walked to the open window and threw the half-inch long cigarette out of the window into the empty air.

A little vermilion spark traced an arc in the air.

She walked back to the box in the corner. A pair of brown-black eyes peered at me from under her hat: "If you don't mind, I want to change my clothes."

"Do you want me to go outside?" I asked.

"No need, just turn your face away." She was already taking off her black velvet coat.

I walked to the window. The October mist was dressing the city in a greyish-white sleeping gown. Two streetlights blinked like yellow eyes.

A few soft rustling sounds, followed by a shoe being dropped on the floor, then another.

"Okay, sorry to bother you."

I turned around. She had already taken off her hat and changed into casual blue velvet clothes, her chest open, revealing the scarlet camisole underneath, and slippers on her feet.

For the first time, I saw two brown-black eyeballs in her small face.

Her dark blue figure framed by a patch of red under her chin, I laughed and said,

"You look just like a swallow with that patch of red under your chin!"

She smiled and started to fasten the buttons on her chest. "He liked me wearing this red shirt. There are many hobbies that you men have that we don't understand. Don't you think so?"

I nodded and picked up my hat. I said, "Mary might be back soon. I have to go." She looked at me:

"Can you tell me where you live?" I took out the "Black Cat Brand" cigarettes I had just bought from my pocket, tore off a little paper, wrote the address on it, and handed it to her with the cigarettes.

"Thank you." She walked me to the door. "When I first saw you, I knew you and I were the same kind of person. Do you believe he will come back?"

I said, "I believe it, I believe it."

I put on my hat, sighed silently, and left.

×　×　×

The next evening, after handling the funeral arrangements for a lonely friend who had been sick for seven months, I did not go to the small restaurant for dinner, and did not return to my apartment until two o'clock in the morning.

After getting out of the car, the White Russian night watchman saw me from the glass door, stood up and opened the door for me.

"GoodNightSirl"

"GOODNightl" I touched my hat.

I got into the elevator, and the elevator operator said, "You're back, sir."

I said, "I'm back."

The elevator took me to the seventh floor. Seeing me return, the No. 11 tea boy greeted me and said:

"Sir, a female guest came to see you tonight."

"What's her name?" I asked. I never had a female guest come to see me.

"She didn't say. She waited for a long time and left a letter."

He handed me a letter.

Looking at the unfamiliar, clumsy handwriting on the public envelope, I tore it open with a "嗤" sound.

Written on the stationery in slanting pencil strokes: "I came to see you. Why didn't you come to dinner? This afternoon I found him on the street, but he ignored me. Do you believe he will come back? I still believe it! Swallow."

"Suicide" and "Being Killed" 224

— Xuan

Today, after reading Yu Dafu's "On Death and Suicide, Love Suicide, and the Like" published in this journal, I thought of the suicide incidents of Japanese people that I saw in Japanese newspapers. It was three years ago when I was in Kyoto, Japan, that I saw an astonishing suicide event reported in the Osaka Mainichi Shimbun. The deceased was a man with a family and property, neither for love failure nor for bankruptcy in speculation, but simply because he was sick and felt that he could no longer live as a healthy person, so he took the means of suicide. He first killed his wife and one son and one daughter (the wife's suicide was probably agreed upon), and this person suffering from a chronic disease locked the door of his house, went to the bank to withdraw a portion of his savings, roamed for a month, and then called his brother who was working in the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Tokyo, explaining the "tragedy" of his whole family, and then he himself committed suicide next to the corpses of his wife and children.

This is a kind of suicide with an abnormal psychology, but behind the abnormal psychology, we see a healthy heart jumping there: this is the serious and earnest attitude towards life, without the slightest willingness to be perfunctory! Since one cannot live as a healthy person, since one cannot fulfill the obligations that healthy people should fulfill, then one might as well commit suicide! ! ! It was this touching will of unwillingness to waste one's life that drove this chronically ill person with a family and property onto the road of suicide!

I curse suicide. However, I am only moved by the suicide of this chronically ill person! Can we criticize such a serious attitude towards life? If he did not have that incurable chronic disease, then he must have been a very brave warrior in the struggle of life, right? If a nation has such a serious attitude towards life, this nation must be inviolable, right?

It is not only the Japanese nation that has this serious and earnest attitude towards life; I just happened to give an example of a Japanese person. Moreover, we should not misunderstand that the Japanese imperialist's barbarous military aggression has any causal relationship with the Japanese people's serious attitude towards life. No! Those are completely two different things! But conversely, a nation without this serious attitude towards life cannot avoid being invaded and not daring to resist, often crying out national humiliation but only having five minutes of enthusiasm. The general middle class in our society who call themselves the backbone are the most lacking in that serious and earnest attitude towards life! Therefore, the funds for the reconstruction of the Zhabei disaster area must be raised by means of lotteries, so relief for Northeastern refugees must be done by holding variety shows, and using movie stars, dancers, and famous prostitutes to call for donations! Therefore, only the poor and suffering people who have always been despised are resisting Japanese imperialism in the freezing cold!

A serious and earnest attitude towards life, without the slightest willingness to live in ease! If one cannot righteously be a person useful to society and mankind, then one might as well die! If one cannot righteously live a rational human life, then one might as well fight to the death! This should be our banner, our creed!

Because those who live in a drunken dream will sooner or later "be killed" even if they are unwilling to "commit suicide"!

On Veneration of Foolishness 225

— Qifan

The blessings of foolish people have long been discovered by predecessors, and some people are very envious of them. The view that "knowing words is the beginning of worries in life" contains this tendency. But in these words, there is still a hidden boast that one is superior to the foolish masses, without knowing the various virtues of foolish people, nor ever thinking that foolishness can indeed be venerated. Therefore, although one is envious of foolish people, one is still unwilling to be a foolish person oneself, so these words become a general empty phrase. What is even more ridiculous is that those who consider themselves intelligent, knowing the pitiable nature of their own situation, still cast a pitying eye on foolish people, in order to satisfy their sense of superiority and to numb themselves.

Foolish people do not know anything. They certainly do not care whether others pity them or envy them, nor do they know what their own situation and position are. All they can see are the things in front of them. They lack foresight, they have no plans or programs, they only know how to do things, and to implement them in a practical and realistic manner. They never consider whether things are dangerous or have no hope of success; they do not do things after predicting that they will definitely succeed, because they have no concern for success and failure. The resistance to Japan by the volunteer armies in various parts of the Northeast is an expression of this kind of foolish spirit.

Slightly intelligent people will never use a few thousand people with insufficient supplies and dilapidated equipment to confront the military power of the entire country of Japan. Very intelligent people would never dare to engage in a short battle with Japanese soldiers with hundreds of thousands of soldiers. People of great wisdom and great intelligence will naturally not act rashly without a 10% chance of winning. Foolish people cannot see this at all. Their failures are also self-inflicted. Fortunately, they do not regard one or a few failures as a great shame and humiliation. Their foolishness enables them to continue to work hard on these unfinished matters. The so-called "hard work, reckless work, stupid work, desperate work until the end" is the consistent spirit of foolishness.

The word "foolish" is often followed by the word "stubborn." Foolish without being stubborn does not constitute foolishness. Only when one is foolish to the point of being incorrigible can one have the true value of foolishness. Some scientists spend their entire lives studying the ecology of a parasite, some scientists spend their entire lives observing the movement of a planet, and some scientists spend decades of effort inventing the use of a gear. It is really not worth it when you think about it, but the preciousness of foolishness lies in this.

In our country, there are too many intelligent people and too few foolish people, so there are only more leaders, alliance leaders, masters, and patriarchs in all aspects, and a lack of believers and implementers. As a result, it has caused wars between leaders and alliance leaders, and enemies between patriarchs and masters, with hundreds of disputes arising before anything is accomplished.

If these people were originally intelligent and had the talents of leaders and alliance leaders, then there would still be something to say, and it would not be a complete injustice. It is a pity that these heads, brains, tops, and elites in China are not necessarily all inherently extremely intelligent. On the contrary, there are indeed many who are very foolish and clumsy, but they also pretend to be very serious and boast of themselves, resulting in hundreds of jokes and a muddle-headed mess, which is really a bit tragic.

To change this shortcoming, the only way is to promote the method of venerating foolishness. In the past, we were too disrespectful to foolish people, so everyone wanted to become intelligent people. As a result, there were too many intelligent people, and things became stagnant. Now, the only way is to raise the position of foolishness above intelligence, hoping that those who are not originally intelligent will continue to do foolish work, and also hoping that those who are originally intelligent will participate in a little foolish work. If this is the case, then it can be hoped that there will be fewer leaders and talents in society who talk empty words and boast, and more implementers who seek truth from facts, and then gradually form a glimmer of dawn for the future. 12.25

Cosmic Rays 226

— Haitian

A new natural phenomenon has attracted people's attention for many years. This is "cosmic rays." Many scientists who study it do not yet have a consistent opinion. However, regarding the source of this mysterious light, everyone seems to agree that it comes from outside the Earth, not from the Earth itself. As for the nature of this light, from what place or what direction it is emitted, whether it comes from other stars, or from within our own solar system, these questions still need to be researched for some time.

Cosmic rays are stronger than X-rays. Thick lead plates that X-rays cannot penetrate can be penetrated by cosmic rays. It can also penetrate deep into lakes. Scientists have put the most sophisticated instruments into the lake to capture this cosmic radiation. It can only not be captured at the very bottom of the lake. Deep water can block the path of cosmic rays, so people speculate that the thick layer of air surrounding the Earth must also absorb it considerably. The higher one goes into the sky, the stronger the cosmic radiation should be.

This summer, Belgian scientist Professor Piccard ascended into the stratosphere at 53,600 feet in a balloon, hoping to measure stronger cosmic radiation than on the Earth's surface below the air layer. But contrary to his and many other scientists' expectations, there was no perceived increase, but rather it seemed to decrease somewhat. Piccard believes that air is the medium of light. The light and heat from the sun must pass through the medium of air in order to emit light and heat. In a vacuum, light and heat have no effect. Therefore, there is less cosmic radiation in the high sky than on the Earth's surface.

What is the use of cosmic rays is not yet known. Thousands of years ago, the ancients rubbed amber to produce small sparks, but unexpectedly this was the electricity of modern civilization. After we know the nature of cosmic rays, they may be more useful than electricity.

Impressions of Suzhou 227

— Zhenfu

(1) Suzhou, A Dream of Three Lives of Flowers and Plants

The two words "Suzhou" have been lingering in my mind for a very long time. What a lovely term this is! What a term that makes people love and admire it! When we think of these two words, we immediately associate them with the character "Xi" on the Gusu Terrace, Yuan Yuan by the Hengtang River, what a glamorous view of Guanqian Street, and how wonderful is the towering Tianping Mountain; it has its swirling scenery in history, and even more dreams that make people love and admire in name. As the saying goes, "Above there is heaven, below there are Suzhou and Hangzhou," if we only look at its bright side, this may be believable, right?

I remember when I was a child, I once traveled with my father on a small inland river steamer. One of the passengers on the ship was an old lady from Suzhou. Although Father Time ruthlessly deprived her of her youthful beauty, and her forehead was carved with deep lines of wrinkles made by the axe of time, the amazing, moving, and endearing features were still maintained on this old lady. When she spoke, a gentle and slow, Suzhou accent with a special style was still maintained. When I heard her speak for the first time, how amazed and delighted I was to listen to this lovely accent, as lovely as music? This was the first time I heard a Suzhou person speak. Even after more than ten years now, I still cannot forget it, how great her magic is! This is not just my boasting. Isn't the "soft language of Wu" recognized by society?

Yuan is my closest classmate, and he is exactly "A Nong was born and grew up in Suzhou," which of course made me even more fond of him. Since I had a deep friendship with Yuan, I have had a personal understanding of Suzhou people, which has further increased my love for Suzhou. Once, in a poem I gave to Yuan, there were two lines: "A kind of gentleness passed down from the Qiantang River, a dream of three lives of beauty to Suzhou," the previous line was thinking of my friends in my hometown, and the next line refers to Yuan. Later, when I read Gong Ding'an's poems, there were several love poems for a Suzhou woman, although he was vaguely unwilling to say it clearly. One of them is "A dream of three lives of flowers and plants to Suzhou," which coincides with my poem; it can also be seen that Suzhou does have a place that makes people love and admire it, not just my ravings. What follows is a reminiscence of my faint impressions of this trip to Suzhou.

(2) Ancient Sites in Withered Landscape Mourning Tiger Hill

I was actually visiting the "Suzhou that I love but cannot see, scratching my head and hesitating" with Yuan as my guide. What a comforting thing this is! When we asked for leave from school, the sky was cloudy and gloomy, but the smile in our hearts was not dampened by it; we were not afraid that the sky would rain and stop our travel mood, even if it really rained, we would travel in the rain, and there would be a special kind of charm that others would not want to appreciate. We were moving forward quickly with this mentality. We took the afternoon train from Wuxi, arrived at Suzhou Station, got off the train, and then went along the railway to Tiger Hill.

On the road: the not very wide streets, the old-fashioned houses, the children's works painted on the walls saying "Down with So-and-So," are not very different from my hometown; no, they are almost the same as the situations everywhere, but a few ancestral halls and a few stone memorial archways indicate that this is a place of outstanding people and spirits. This is the situation outside Suzhou City, which still preserves the original Chinese appearance and has not been modernized. When the yellow walls and the golden and brilliant title plaque of the Tiger Hill Temple shone into our eyes, our destination had arrived. We walked into the temple gate, and there were many trees on both sides, already with some desolate artistic conception, indicating that it was already late autumn. In the midst of weeds and overgrown grass, there are many tombs, isolated pavilions, and broken steles. If we explore them from a historical perspective, there may be many touching and lamentable things contained in them, but we are just tourists who have come for the sake of enjoyment, so naturally we have no time to verify them for him. On the left, there is a newly built pavilion with a stone tablet erected, recording the story of a filial son named Zhang who was burned to death while saving his mother. There are inscriptions by famous people from Suzhou. This filial son Zhang was a poor Jiangbei person, a Jiangbei person who was despised by people, but he was able to occupy a place in this famous Tiger Hill and be worshiped. The filial son in the ground can also be comforted. (To be continued)

The Crossroads of the Era and Love, Part 27 228

— Zhang Ziping

"Nonsense! No manners at all! Luckily, Mr. Lin and Mr. Liao are not strangers."

"Wife and slave are not synonyms! Mr. Liao! Right?"

Madam Cao stretched her neck, tilted her head, made a half-grimace, and went to the other side. Cao Haiquan thought, this is truly a modern woman.

In the end, it was still because the revolution had not yet succeeded, and a woman is still a woman. Madam Cao finally succumbed to Cao Shiguang. She came to the church alone and returned from the church alone.

After watching his wife's lonely figure disappear, Cao Shiguang turned his head towards Lin and Liao as if completely numb.

"Let's go."

"But I'm not free at eight o'clock."

Haiquan quickly stated.

"Is there anything important? Why don't we have a good time tonight?"

"I have an appointment at eight o'clock, I can't break my promise."

"It doesn't matter."

"How is it that you in the religious world don't value credit?"

"It's just hanging up a signboard."

Cao Shiguang's attitude was quite innocent and straightforward, only Liao Haifeng remained silent.

"Although I haven't been baptized, I must keep my word."

Haiquan said with a smile.

"Mr. Lin is right."

Mr. Liao also smiled.

"Then, let's go to the restaurant first. There's still an hour and a half, is there not enough time?"

Cao Shiguang paid for the tram fare from the church to the S restaurant on K Road. They ordered a two-dollar set meal at the restaurant. Originally, everyone was a bit hungry, and eating would have been fine. Cao Shiguang kept clamoring to drink old wine, so they ordered half a catty of aged Hua Diao. He poured and drank it himself.

After a while, the food was finished. The waiter brought three hot towels.

"Lao Cao, let me make a phone call to check on that matter."

Mr. Liao took the towel, wiped his mouth, and walked out. Cao Shiguang held the hot towel, wiped his face, and then carefully wiped his hands. A black mark had already stained the snow-white towel.

"Lao Lin, please sit for a while, I'll go take a leak."

He walked inside.

China Has Too Few Madmen 229

— Zhi

Why do we study, to become officials? To get rich? True, our parents probably want us to graduate from school! High school graduates are like Xiucai, middle school graduates are like Juren, and university graduates are like Hanlin, just like in the Qing Dynasty imperial examination era, seeking golden houses in officialdom. But we, the young and determined, will never somersault in this evil thought. However, in today's society, most people believe that becoming an official is the best shortcut to a comfortable life. Since humans tend to seek pleasure and avoid suffering, and since humans tend to choose less labor and more comfort, and since becoming an official is a very profitable business, how is it possible to prevent people from tending towards it? Look at Zhang San, who was originally a teacher in a primary school, earning only a little over ten yuan a month, not enough to support his parents or raise his wife and children. Friends and relatives all regarded him as a useless person, looked down on him, and ridiculed him, causing him to lose the joy of life. So he became indignant, abandoned his pen and joined the army. Before long, he graduated from a military academy, and went to work in a certain army. He immediately wore a small leather belt on his shoulder, and tied leggings around his legs, looking like a proud military officer! So this one called him Battalion Commander, that one called him Sir. Relatives respected him, friends admired him. Although what he learned was the game of feeding cannons with flesh, and what he did was harming others without benefiting himself, he earned gold and silver every month. From then on, his parents were addressed as Old Master and Old Madam, and his wife was addressed as Madam. Not only did he not have to worry about food and clothing, but he could also join the ranks of the wealthy! Who wouldn't envy him? Look at Li Si, he was originally a cunning rogue, who made a living by deception all day long. But because the times are times that create heroes, those with heroic talents will naturally enter the realm of heroes, Long live so-and-so! Down with so-and-so! Look! He is now a formidable big shot! When the army came, the locality was ravaged, the people were slaughtered, and society was in chaos, but his destiny had been made! So Mr. Li also became a meritorious servant of society. From then on, he could glorify his ancestors, live in Western-style houses, ride in cars, eat delicacies, and embrace beautiful concubines. Who wouldn't want to taste such heavenly bliss? To be honest, in this world, what better business is there than getting promoted and getting rich? You want others to embark on the path of knowledge with more suffering than joy, only madmen will listen to you!

Is this truly everyone's feeling? True, most of the smart people in the world think this way, but we must know that madmen are the driving force that propels the wheels of society forward. The progress of modern society has all been created by a few madmen. Think about it, the person who invented pottery burned all the furniture in his house, even the bed he slept on, for experimental purposes. Isn't this the behavior of a madman? The person who invented the airplane made some gadgets, sat on them himself, braved the danger, and soared in the air like a bird. Isn't this the behavior of a madman? Those who study knowledge bury themselves in the laboratory all day long, from youth to old age, and all they get is a few truths that ordinary people think are insignificant. How can they compare to high officials whose doors are crowded and whose names are resounding? This is naturally also a madman! The rest, such as explorers and revolutionaries who disregard their lives, needless to say, are madmen! Ladies and gentlemen! Where is the reason for China's backwardness? It's because there are too few madmen and too many smart people!

Santa Claus's Gifts 230

— A Jie

Santa Claus probably understands "the philosophy of life": So every year when the cold winter season of Christmas comes, the old man, dressed in red, braves the snow, and is sure to bring many gifts to give to people: candy, cakes, toys: he carries a big bag full of them, hunches his back, and stumbles to the world to give gifts. Foreigners are very happy on this Christmas holiday!! Especially children, who hold banquets and celebrate Christmas: they light candles on the tree, which look like trees of fire and silver flowers, very bright and pleasing to the eye, and are called "Christmas Trees." On this day, they eat turkey and beef, which they call "Holy Meat:" they drink wine, which they call "Holy Blood:" they sing and dance, spending this Christmas night in great revelry! During our Chinese Winter Solstice, everyone eats tangyuan and rice cakes to get a good omen: at night, there is also the superstition of seeking dreams. The customs of the East and West are different after all.

I think our countrymen, sleep on that day

Page 16

of the night, | Winter Solstice Night | are sure to have dreams. But dreams are different for everyone. Most people must dream of golden ingots rolling into their arms. Perhaps some people dream of becoming officials, ordering people around, being full of prestige, having beautiful wives and concubines, fertile fields and luxurious houses, and achieving the goal of wealth and status. Some are dreaming of buying up enemy goods, and their business is booming, and they are about to get rich, when suddenly a bomb comes and awakens their good dream. Perhaps some young people are dreaming of embracing their lovers, making vows of eternal love, and being very sweet, when suddenly a rival in love comes, pulls out a pistol, aims at them, and all they hear is a "bang" in their ears, scaring them awake, and it turns out to be a dream of Nanke.·······

Our countrymen, after having "Winter Solstice Illusions," are followed by the foreign Winter Solstice, | Christmas | that tactless Santa Claus, who is going to give gifts again. What are Santa Claus's gifts? They are neither candy, nor toys, nor the ruthless bombs of the ××× group, but a warm conscience. Santa Claus gives this because our countrymen lack this thing; therefore, they don't put the country in their hearts, and don't care whether the country is destroyed, only knowing to desperately buy enemy goods, import enemy goods, cause trouble, and bring disaster upon themselves: so he doesn't send other things, only this warm conscience. I wonder if our compatriots like to accept it?

Alas! Santa Claus! Why did you give the Northeast Three Provinces to the Japanese as a gift? We have accepted your gift of conscience, and we still have to snatch this gift back from their hands. Everyone, get up quickly!

Just a Casual Chat 231

— Chi · Fo ·

Life is like a journey through the desert, with more hurricanes and less water and grass: it is only meaningful if people can resist the hurricanes and find water and grass.

Life is like playing cards. Getting good cards is like being born into a wealthy family. Getting bad cards is like being born into a poor family. If you are a friend with empty hands at home, even if you try your best, you might be able to make a big hand, but it's very difficult after all! Also, the nouveau riche, the rich who get rich by improper means, are like friends with a living hand, making a big hand.

The wealthy old men live in seclusion, and although they have grand mansions, what is the difference between them and the taste of iron windows? When they go out, with cars in front and behind, and bodyguards on the left and right, aren't they like police and soldiers monitoring robbers?

Once he died, more than a dozen beautiful concubines each went their separate ways, and each only received two thousand several hundred yuan. I wonder what the friends who specialize in extortion think about this?

A Random Writing 232

— Rui Yucheng

I heard that Minister ×× recently bought several police dogs in the United States, worth about several thousand yuan: and also hired two teachers for them, who train them all day long: the teachers' monthly salary is also several hundred yuan each. After hearing this, I dare not believe it's true: if it is true, then it really is "it is better to be a dog than a man!"

The government's proposition is to first secure the internal situation and then deal with external enemies. Now that the communist bandits have been pacified, I think they will soon swear an oath to march out of the customs. As long as they are determined to resist, why fear the Japanese invaders!

There used to be a four-character couplet, called "Soil can produce gold, the land does not begrudge treasures:" I didn't expect that both sentences have now become a reality. Now that ×× is publicly sold, isn't it soil producing gold? Not recovering the lost land, isn't that the land not begrudging treasures?

Now, to fall in love, there must be two prerequisite questions: First, "Do you have money?" Second, "Are you beautiful?" All other knowledge and character are irrelevant. I'm just afraid that poor and ugly people will not be able to marry wives in the future, and will have to embrace bachelorhood permanently.

The law clearly stipulates that having illicit relations with a woman under the age of twenty should be a crime; but in society, there are often formal marriages with teenage girls, why isn't this considered a crime?

It is most difficult to be a person in society. If you are humble to others, some people will say you are flattering; if you are arrogant to others, some people will say you are conceited; if your clothes are gorgeous, they will say you are extravagant; if you dress shabbily: they will say you are poor and cold: Absolutely strictly speaking, it is impossible to find a person who suits everyone's wishes.

When you see someone riding in a car, even if you have no relatives or friends, you can recognize them as relatives and friends: when you see three beggars, even if they are really your uncles, you will definitely treat them as strangers.

No matter what organization, the more money you get, the more leisurely your work must be; the less money you get, the more laborious your work is.
